wscroll = new NvScroll(); wscroll.name = "wscroll"; wscroll.height = 25; wscroll.width = 99; wscroll.scrollspeed = 1; wscroll.pausedelay = 3000; wscroll.pausemouseover = false;

		var wscroll_stopped_by_keyboard = false;
		var wscroll_stopped_by_mouse = false;


		function wscroll_stop_keyboard()
		{
			if(!wscroll_stopped_by_mouse){
				wscroll.stop = true;
				wscroll_stopped_by_keyboard = true;
			}
		}

		function wscroll_start_keyboard()
		{
			if(!wscroll_stopped_by_mouse){
				wscroll.stop = false;
				wscroll_stopped_by_keyboard = false;
			}
		}

		function nvweather (num, name, temp, img, url, desc ) {

			return "<li id=wscrollitem"+num+" style='left:0px; width:"+wscroll.width+"; position:absolute; top:"+wscroll.height*num+"px'; title='서울 18.0&deg;C\n수원 18.0&deg;C\n인천 19.0&deg;C\n춘천 19.0&deg;C\n강릉 18.0&deg;C\n청주 18.0&deg;C\n대전 19.0&deg;C\n대구 25.0&deg;C\n부산 22.0&deg;C\n전주 17.0&deg;C\n광주 18.0&deg;C\n제주 20.0&deg;C\n'><a href="+url+" id=snb_weather_"+num+"i onfocus=\"wscroll_stop_keyboard();\" onblur=\"wscroll_start_keyboard();\"><img src='"+img+"' width='36' height='26' alt='"+desc+"' title='"+desc+"' >"+name+"<span> <em>"+temp+"</em>&deg;C</span></a></li>";
		}

		
		wscroll.add( nvweather(0,"서울", "18.0", "http://static.naver.net/weather/images/w_icon/w_s18.gif", "http://weather.naver.com/rgn/cityWetrCity.nhn?cityRgnCd=CT001013", "비 끝남") );
		
		wscroll.add( nvweather(1,"수원", "18.0", "http://static.naver.net/weather/images/w_icon/w_s3.gif", "http://weather.naver.com/rgn/cityWetrCity.nhn?cityRgnCd=CT001015", "흐림") );
		
		wscroll.add( nvweather(2,"인천", "19.0", "http://static.naver.net/weather/images/w_icon/w_s3.gif", "http://weather.naver.com/rgn/cityWetrCity.nhn?cityRgnCd=CT001028", "흐림") );
		
		wscroll.add( nvweather(3,"춘천", "19.0", "http://static.naver.net/weather/images/w_icon/w_s4.gif", "http://weather.naver.com/rgn/cityWetrCity.nhn?cityRgnCd=CT003007", "보통비계속") );
		
		wscroll.add( nvweather(4,"강릉", "18.0", "http://static.naver.net/weather/images/w_icon/w_s3.gif", "http://weather.naver.com/rgn/cityWetrCity.nhn?cityRgnCd=CT004001", "흐림") );
		
		wscroll.add( nvweather(5,"청주", "18.0", "http://static.naver.net/weather/images/w_icon/w_s4.gif", "http://weather.naver.com/rgn/cityWetrCity.nhn?cityRgnCd=CT005010", "약한 이슬비") );
		
		wscroll.add( nvweather(6,"대전", "19.0", "http://static.naver.net/weather/images/w_icon/w_s3.gif", "http://weather.naver.com/rgn/cityWetrCity.nhn?cityRgnCd=CT006005", "흐림") );
		
		wscroll.add( nvweather(7,"대구", "25.0", "http://static.naver.net/weather/images/w_icon/w_s3.gif", "http://weather.naver.com/rgn/cityWetrCity.nhn?cityRgnCd=CT007007", "흐림") );

	function wscroll_stop_mouse()
	{
		if(!wscroll_stopped_by_keyboard){
			wscroll.stop = true;
			wscroll_stopped_by_mouse = true;
		}
	}

	function wscroll_start_mouse()
	{
		if(!wscroll_stopped_by_keyboard){
			wscroll.stop = false;
			wscroll_stopped_by_mouse = false;
		}
	}

	var pathname = location.pathname;
	var search = location.search;

	function getUrlListToActivate(lnbMenuInfo) {
		var result = [];
		var targetUrl = lnbMenuInfo.url;
		result.push(targetUrl);

		var urlListToActivate = [];
		var onUrl = $.trim(lnbMenuInfo.onUrl);
		if (onUrl.length > 0) {
			urlListToActivate = onUrl.split(";");
			result = result.concat(urlListToActivate);
		}

		if (lnbMenuInfo.subMenuList) {
			for (var i = 0; i < lnbMenuInfo.subMenuList.length; i++) {
				var subMenu = lnbMenuInfo.subMenuList[i];
				result.push(subMenu.url);

				var onUrl = $.trim(subMenu.onUrl);
				if (onUrl.length > 0) {
					result = result.concat(onUrl.split(";"));
				}
			}
		}


		return result;
	}

	function hasQueryParameterToActivate(urlToActivate, currentQueryParameter) {
		var queryParameterToActivate = getURLParameter(urlToActivate);
		var currentQueryParameter = getURLParameter(currentQueryParameter);

		if (!queryParameterToActivate || !currentQueryParameter) {
			return;
		}

		var queryParameterToActivateMap = changeQueryStringToObject(queryParameterToActivate);
		var currentQueryParameterMap = changeQueryStringToObject(currentQueryParameter);

		for (var i in queryParameterToActivateMap) {
			for (var j in currentQueryParameterMap) {
				if (i == j && queryParameterToActivateMap[i] == currentQueryParameterMap[j]) {
					return true;
				}
			}
		}

		return false;
	}

	function getMenuIdx(lnbMenuInfoList) {
		var foundMenuIdx = -1;

		for (var i = 0; i < lnbMenuInfoList.length; i++) {
			var lnbMenuInfo = lnbMenuInfoList[i];
			var urlListToActivate = getUrlListToActivate(lnbMenuInfo);

			for (var j = 0; j < urlListToActivate.length; j++) {
				var urlToActivate = urlListToActivate[j];

				if (urlToActivate == pathname) {
					foundMenuIdx = i;
				} else if (urlToActivate.indexOf(pathname) >= 0) {
					if (hasQueryParameterToActivate(urlToActivate, search)) {
						foundMenuIdx = i;
					}
				}
			}
		}


		return foundMenuIdx;
	}

	function setTopMenu() {
		var foundTopMenuIndex = getMenuIdx(lnbMenuInfoList);
		if (foundTopMenuIndex != -1) {
			var lnbMenuInfo = lnbMenuInfoList[foundTopMenuIndex];
			$("#lnbTopMenu_" + foundTopMenuIndex).addClass("on");
			$("#lnbTopMenuImage_" + foundTopMenuIndex).attr("src", lnbMenuInfo.on);
			$("#lnbSubMenu_" + foundTopMenuIndex).show();

			if (lnbMenuInfo.subMenuList.length) {
				$("#lnb_main_sub").addClass("lnbsub");
			} else {
				$("#lnb_main_sub").removeClass("lnbsub");
			}
		}

		return foundTopMenuIndex;
	}

	function setSubMenu(topMenuIdx) {
		var lnbMenuInfo = lnbMenuInfoList[topMenuIdx];
		if (!lnbMenuInfo.subMenuList.length) {
			return;
		}

		var foundSubMenuIndex = getMenuIdx(lnbMenuInfo.subMenuList);
		if (foundSubMenuIndex != -1) {
			var focusedSubMenuImg = $("#lnbSubMenu_" + topMenuIdx + "_" + foundSubMenuIndex).find("img");
			focusedSubMenuImg.attr("src", lnbMenuInfo.subMenuList[foundSubMenuIndex].on);
			focusedSubMenuImg.after("<span class=\"blind\">선택됨</span>");
			focusedSubMenuImg.after("<span class=\"check\"></span>");
		}
	}

	var topMenuIdx = setTopMenu();
	if(topMenuIdx >= 0){
		setSubMenu(topMenuIdx);
	}

	function goToMobileUrl(mobileRedirectUrl) {
		if(mobileRedirectUrl) {
			location.href = "/mobileview.nhn?url=" + encodeURIComponent(mobileRedirectUrl);
		}else{
			location.href = "/index.nhn";
		}
	}
